5.1.1.1 hariþ oü
priyatàü bhagavàn viùõus sarva-deve÷varo hariþ
÷rãvatsàïkas[*1] sahasràkùas sahasra-caraõas tathà
5.1.1.2 jitan te puõóarãkàkùa namas te vi÷va-bhàvana
namas te 'stu hçùãke÷a mahà-puruùa pårva-ja
5.1.1.3 bhavantu sarvàþ[*2] puõyàkhyà nimittà÷ ÷obhanànvitàþ
tvat-prasàdàd vayaü viùõo tava dàsàs samàgatàþ
5.1.1.4 sàdhayàmo vimànaü te prasàdaü kuru no bhavàn
sàhàyyaü sarva-bhçtyàs te kurvantu tava ÷àsanàt
5.1.1.5 ÷ànta-vã÷àri-bhåtàdãn[*3] visçjàsmàbhir eva tu
anapàyã prayàtv agre chitvà vighnaü punaþ-punaþ
[*1] Irregular bahu-vrãhi accentuation.  cf.  A Vedic Grammar for Students, A.A. MacDonell, page 455a.
[*2] Underlined syllables receive a "double svarita," two parallel vertical lines above the syllable, in the published text.
[*3] cf.  Kà÷yapa J¤àna Kàõóaþ, chapter 34, vã÷a-hãne ripu-vçddhiþ.

5.1.0.5 manyamàno bhavanàya kalpita(g)ü sapta ca

5.1.16.1 ime bãjà vrãhi-yavà ruhantåùõàü÷u-prasàdàt
somenàrpità grahair nirvyàdhikà÷ ÷uddhà÷ ÷ubhà bhavantu
5.1.16.2 praroha-bãjàn nirvapàmi bhåmau ye brahma-sçùñà da÷a sapta caiva.  te vardhità vçùñi-va÷ena sarve saüpàlyamànà hy amçtena lokàn
5.1.16.3 sapta gràmyàs sapta càraõyakà÷ ca ye gharma-naùñà hima-varùa-sçùñàs te vçùñi-bhåtà hy amçtaü rakùantu
5.1.16.4 dãrõàrdra-saü÷uùka-vivardhamànà målaiþ phalai÷ ÷àkais samçddha[*30]-råpaiþ
annena martyànàü[*31] haviùà suràõàn te vai ruhantàü tçõavat pa÷ubhyaþ
5.1.16.5 tàn bhåmi-÷uddhyai nirvapàmi bãjàn deva-sthiti-kàraõàya
5.1.16.6 ye vyoma-bhåmy-agni[*32]-jalasya vàyos saüyoga-bhåtàþ praruhanti sarve
tàn daivike ÷uddhi-karàya bãjàn nirvapàmi deva-sthiti-kàraõàya
[*30] 1946 edition shows the incorrect reading pamçddhaiþ which was corrected in the 1984 edition.  In Telegu script, pa and sa are very similar.
[*31] 1946 text reads martyànü.  The 1984 text reads martyàn, assuming that what appears to be a second r is actually a symbol for final n with one loop broken off.  Otherwise as it stands, the 1984 edition would read marrtyà.  I have corrected all these unintelligible forms to martyànàü, which combined with annena provides an intelligible reading parallel to haviùà suràõàn.
[*32] The text places an anudatta under the å of bhåmy and then a svarita over the a in agni, seemingly an impossible feat of recitation.



5.1.17.1 yad bãja-bhåtam idam antarikùaü, yad bãjaü càgniþ pçthivã rasa÷ ca tad bãja-rohàya vahantu vàtàs, saüvardhamànà ruhantàü prarohàþ
5.1.17.2 nirãtikàs te bahavo ruhantas saüpàlyamànà hy amçta-vàyunà ca
kàlena bãjàþ praruhanti coptà bãjàd ahaü pracariùyàmi dharmam
5.1.17.3 ete bãjà rasa-bhåtà vahantu somena sçùñà amçtavat pa÷ubhyaþ
etàn prarohàn rasa-bhåta-jàtàn dattàn me bhuktvà pracarantu gàvaþ
5.1.17.4 tasmàn mamaitàn pravapàmi gehe te me pa÷ånàm amçtà vahantu
etaü stutà me pravahantv amutra te puõya-loke mama deha-bhåtàþ
5.1.17.5 samudravatã ÷çïge-÷çïge

5.1.19.1 pçùñho rudra çùayo romàõy uro guhas tãrthà làïgålam
kukùir medinã cakùuùã candràdityau vàlà vidyàdharàþ
5.1.19.2 ådhas sàgaràþ[*35] stanà nadyo gàtraü bhå-dharàþ
asthãni parvatà rudhiraü mitrà-varuõau màüsam agnir jàhnavã måtram
5.1.19.3 khura uragà jyeùñhà[*36] nàsikà dantà marutaþ
jihvà sarasvatã karõaþ kavãndra÷ ÷akçt puõya-de÷am[*37]
5.1.19.4 etàs sa-vatsà gàvas sa-vçùàþ
yathà-sukhaü carantu kàmaü carantàm
yathà-sukhaü vrajantu kàmaü vrajantàm
yathà-sukhaü mudantu kàmaü mudantàm
5.1.19.5 gàvo hi me màtaras santu sarvà me go-vçùàþ pitaraþ santu sarve
vatsà mama bhràtara eva santu tasmàd iëà ÷uddhi-karà bhavantu
5.1.19.6 imàü si¤càmãmàm anugacchàmãmàü ÷odhayàmãmàü mudantu devà vitatà vare÷àm[*38]
5.1.19.7 bhu¤jantu dattaü balim adya vãrà÷
÷vaþ ÷ràvaye[*39] yåyam a÷eùam asmàd
gacchadhvam àryàs su-manasà ca yuktàþ
[*33] Normal accent duhatàü.
[*34] I read this as dharà sà yà.  In his English translation of the KJK, Goudriaan (p. 319) lists an alternative reading dhàràyàsàya from a group of manuscripts which he calls L.  Goudriaan is unable to translate these letters either as dhàràsàyà (which he incorrectly lists as dhàràsàya) or as dhàràyàsàya.
[*35] I have added visarga to correct the text.
[*36] The 1946 edition correctly gives jyeùñhà, however the 1984 edition has corrupted the word to jeùñhà.
[*37] The older edition correctly gives puõya-, however the 1984 edition of the text has corrupted it to çuõya-.  In Telegu script, p and ç, when following a consonant, are similar.
[*38] The text gives the unintelligible vareëàm, which I have changed to vare÷àm, to the (female) lord of boons.  I chose this over the possible vareùàm since in the Telegu script ë is very similar to ÷.  Also the reading of vare÷àm gives provides a referent for the four occurrences in this text of imàm.
[*39] I have corrected ÷va÷ràvaye to ÷vaþ ÷ràvaye.  Thus the word ÷vaþ, "tomorrow" follows the word adya, "today" in the previous line, a common sequence.  cf. RV 6.56.6d.

[*62] The 1984 Telegu script edition of the VMP has accidentally put pages 17 and 18 of the first pra÷na after page 16 of the fifth pra÷na.  Similarly page 17 and 18 of the fifth pra÷na has been put after page 16 of the first pra÷na.  The first four pra÷nas form a single book and pra÷nas 5-8 form the second book.  Therefore the text begins numbering again from 1 at the beginning of pra÷na 5, and this is why the two sets of pages 17 and 18 were confused.

[*246] Beginning with this verse and ending with verse 5.1.154.1, àvaha devàn yajamànàya, is a set of pratãkas which are found in TS 2.5.9.1-4.  The complete verse is as follows (I have underlined the Sanskrit and English that appears in the VMP text): agne mahàï asãty àha mahàn hy eùa yad agnir bràhmaõety àha bràhmaõo hy eùa bhàratety àhaiùa hi devebhyo havyaü bharati deveddha ity àha devà hy etam aindhate manviddha ity àha manur hy etam uttaro devebhya aindharùi-ùñuta ity àharùayo hy etam astuvan viprànumadita ity àha (1) viprà hy ete yac chu÷ruvàüso brahma-saü÷ita ity àha brahma-saü÷ito hy eùa ghçtahavana ity àha ghçtàhutir hy asya priyatamà praõãr yaj¤ànàm ity àha praõãr hy eùa yaj¤ànàü rathãr adhvaràõàm ity àhaiùa hi deva-ratho 'tårto hotety àha na hy etaü ka÷cana (2) tarati tårõir havya-vàó ity àha sarvaü hy eùa taraty àspàtraü juhår devànàm ity àha juhår hy eùa devànàü camaso deva-pàna ity aha camaso hy eùa deva-pàno 'ràü ivàgne nemir devàüs tvaü paribhår asãty àha devàn hy eùa paribhår yad bråyàd à vaha devàn devayate yajamànàyeti bhràtçvyam asmai (3) janayed à vaha devàn yajamànàyety àha yajamànam evaitena vardhayati... | Keith's translation: "`O Agni, thou art great', he says, for Agni is great.  `O Brahman', he says, for he is a Brahman.  `O Bhàrata', he says, for he bears the sacrifice to the gods.  `Kindled by the gods', he says, for the gods kindled him.  `Kindled by Manu', he says, for Manu kindled him after the gods.  `Praised by the èùis', he says, for the èùis praised him.  `Rejoiced in by sages', he says, for learned people are sages.  `Celebrated by the poets', he says, for learned people are the poets.  `Quickened by the holy power (Brahman)', he says, for he is quickened by the holy power (Brahman).  `With ghee offering', he says, for ghee is his dearest offering.  `Leader of the sacrifices', he says, for he is the leader of the sacrifices.  `Charioteer of the rites', he says, for he is the chariot of the gods.  `The Hotç unsurpassed', he says, for no one surpasses him.  `Surpassing, bearing the oblation', he says, for he surpasses all.  `The mouth dish, the ladle of the gods', he says, for he is the ladle of the gods.  `The bowl from which the gods drink', he says, for he is the bowl from which the gods drink.  `O Agni, like a felly the spokes, thou dost surround the gods', he says, for he surrounds the gods.  If he were to say, `Bring hither the gods to the pious sacrificer', he would produce an enemy for him.  `Bring hither the gods to the sacrificer', he says; verily with that he makes the sacrificer to grow great."
[*247] This verse is in parentheses in the Sanskrit text.

hariþ oü tatth sat

ørã ørã vikhanasa mahà-gurave namaþ
ørã-vaikhànasa-mantra-pra÷nàùñake
úaùñaþ-pra÷na-pràrambhaþ

6.1.1 hariþ oü
6.1.2 ato devà avantu no yato viùõur vicakrame
pçthivyàs sapta-dhàmabhis svàhà
6.1.3 idaü viùõur vi cakrame tredhà ni dadhe padam
samåóham asya pà(g)üsure svàhà
6.1.4 trãõi padà vi cakrame viùõur gopà adàbhyaþ
 [t]ato[*327] dharmàõi dhàrayan svàhà
6.1.5 viùõoþ karmàõi pa÷yata yato vratàni paspa÷e
indrasya yujyas sakhà svàhà
6.1.6 tad viùõoþ paramaü pada(g)ü sadà pa÷yanti sårayaþ
divãva cakùur àtata(gg)ü svàhà
6.1.7 tad vipràso vipanyavo jàgçvàüsas sam indhate
viùõor yat paramaü pada(gg)ü svàhà
